 " On the last day of Sahitya Aaj Tak-2019, writer-writer Manoj Muntashir has decorated the festival of 'sahitya Aaj Tak 2019', the biggest Mahakumbh of literature

 kavita sunne kii cheez nahin he
 
 
 Manoj Muntashir, originally from Amethi Gauriganj, said that poetry is a thing to be read, it is not a thing to be heard, but a love of our culture and listeners, due to which poems are heard today
 faij ahamed faij kii paktiyaan 'bol ki lab aaazaad hai tere' kaa zikr karte hue muntashir ne kaha ki main ye tay nahin kar paaya ki main kaamyaab hum yaa naakaam, lekin jab main manoj shukla se manoj muntashir hua to wo mere liye badi baat thi
 Because i rebelled for poetry
 unhone kaha ki mere pitaaji kisaan he
 6 months work in the fields and 6 months offer prayers and weddings
 aise main gauriganj se mumbai nikalnaa badi chunauti thi

 kyonki unhen lag rahaa tha main kuch dinon baad waapas gauriganj laut aauungaa
 However this did not happen and today i am in Mumbai as Manoj Muntashir

 bahubali ke dialog kaa zikr

 Many times it will happen to you that you will buy a packet of milk from outside and when the next day you go to boil to use it, the milk will burst
 ye bahut hi saamaanya baat he
 In the summer, especially milk and milk products go bad
 aise main ye bahut jaruri ho jaataa he ki hamen doodh or duusare deyari products ko store karne kaa sahi tarika pataa ho
 Usually we keep milk packets, yogurt, cheese and other things in the freeze to think that they are safe but it is not so
 kai baar kuch chijen fries main rakhane ke baavjood kharaab ho jaati hai
 In such a situation, you can keep your dairy products safe by adopting these methods
 1
 Always take care of temperature
 Dairy products should be stored in cool temperature only
 haalankidayari products ko nami se bachaakar hi rakhen
 Keeping in a cool and dry place keeps dairy products and milk perfect for a long time
 isi tarah garm taapmaana main bhi ye chijen aasaani se kharaab ho jaati hai
 Actually, bacteria thrive more in moisture and heat, which causes dairy products to deteriorate
 2
 Use only after boiling
 If you drink milk every day, then make sure that you do not drink milk without boiling
 doodh ko ubalkar pine se isamen maujuud bacteria khatm ho jate hai
 Drinking lukewarm milk is more beneficial than drinking cold milk
 3
 Buy only by looking at the manufacturing date, it not only applies to milk and dairy products, but also to everything that is purchased from outside
 doodh or duusare deyari products kharidte samay hameshaa us par likhi taarikh dekh len

 What is the importance of Shani Dev: The son of Saturn is considered very powerful and has amazing importance in human life
 shani dev mrityulok ke aise swami hai, jo vyakti ke achche-bure karmon ke aadhaar par sajaa dekar unhen sudharne ke liye prerit karte hai

 Justice Ranjan Gogoi, one of the four judges, asked pti-language in Kolkata when asked about the future direction to resolve the crisis that there is no crisis in the Supreme Court
